[2] _rgya gar skad du/_d+hA ki ni sarba tsit+ta spyi ro ta sur+ya gu h+ya tan na ma/_bod skad du/_mkha' 'gro thams cad kyi snying khrag klong gsal 'bar ma nyi ma'i gsang rgyud ces bya ba/_rig stong skye ba med pa'i dbyings/_ye nas lhun gyis grub pa/_rgyar ma chad pa/_phyogs su ma lhung ba/_gang yang ma yin pa/_gang du 'byung ba'i gzhi/_sngar yang sangs ma rgyas pa/_da sangs mi rgya ba/_da lta yang sangs rgyas la mi gnas pa/_sngar 'khor bar ma 'khyams pa/_da 'khor bar mi 'khyams pa/_da lta 'khor ba na mi gnas pa/_lung du ma bstan pa'ang ma yin pa/_kun gyi mkha' rgya/_b+ha ga yangs pa'i klong*/_sra ba/_brtan pa/_mi 'jig pa/_ma 'khrul ba/_mi g.yo ba/_mi 'gyur ba/_phyi der 'dzin gyi rgya ma ral ba/nang 'od lnga'i kha dog ma 'gags pa/_phyi der rtog gi bzo ma grub pa la/_nang mkhyen spyod kyis thugs rje ma yeng bar/_dran pa med bzhin du rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa/_kho rang yin [3]/bzhin du bdag dang bdag gis ma phyes pa/_'khor 'das kun gyi byed las kyi stobs dang ldan kyang /_stobs rtsal de yi rjes su mi 'brang bar/_rang bab gdal ba'i sku de kho na la phyag 'tshal lo/_/oM ma hI ha ri ni sa ra tsa hri ya/_a tri rmi tsit+ta dung dung dza dza/

[CHAPTER 1] _'di skad bdag gis bstan pa'i dus na/_gnas phun sum tshogs pa 'khor 'das kyi spyi dpal b+ha ga yangs par/_ston pa phun sum tshogs pa kun tu bzang mo snang stong bzung ris dang bral ba'i thugs kar bem stong ma yin/_rig stong yin pa'i rtags su/_rdo rje sems dpa' tshon gang bas brgyan nas/_dus snga phyi thog mtha'i rtsis dang bral ba'i dus su/_'khor rang gsal rig pa'i rang rtsal mkha' 'gro ma sde lnga la/_bstan pa rtsol med du/_rgyu 'bras las 'das pa'i don 'di bka' stsal to/_spyits+tsha zlo b+hu:_e ma 'khor 'das thams cad kun/_/ye stong rtsa bral gzhi yin te/_/ma 'gag rtsal snang lam du shar/_/ye grol chen po'i [4] 'bras bu thob/_/'di ru ma 'dus gang yang med/_/ces gsungs pa tsam gyis/_'jig rten gyi khams steng 'og thams cad/_mer mer por gyur to/_/khyom khyom por gyur to/_/'od zer gyis rang bzhin du gyur to/_/'ja' dang /_'od dang /_sgra dang /_zer gyis 'khrigs par gyur nas/_thams cad rang bzhin gzhi snang chen por gsal la 'pho 'gyur med par lhan gyis mnyams par gyur to/_kun tu bzang mo klong gsal 'bar ma nyi ma'i gsang rgyud gsang sngags gnad mdzod las/_gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o//_brda' yig :

[CHAPTER 44] yang ston pas bka' stsal pa/_nyon cig rig pa'i 'khor gdangs rnams// [143] a nu'i theg pa 'di lta ste/_/chos can thams cad thabs yin yab/_/chos nyid thams cad shes rab yum/_/gnyis med bde chen sras su 'dod/_/yang na 'dus byas thabs mchog yab/_/'dus ma byas rnams shes rab yum/_/gnyis med bde chen sras su 'dod/_/lha dang lha mo bskyed mi dgos/_/chu las nya ldang ji bzhin du/_/snying po dran pas chog pa'o/_/chos nyid kun bzang yum mkha' la/_/chos sku kun bzang yab gsang bstod/_/gnyis med bde chen sras su 'dod/_/lam der mthar phyin 'bras bu la//_phung po khams dang skye mched dang*/_gnas gyur sku dang ye shes te/_/dug lnga gnas gyur ye shes lnga/_/rgyas par sgyu 'phrul dra bar shes/_/rab ni tshe gcig sangs rgyas thob/_/'bring ni 'chi khar dbyings dang 'dres/_/tha mar bar dor longs sku thob/_/de yang theg pa'i lam stegs yin/_/kun bzang b+ha ga'i klong du shar/_/ma spang rol pa'i rgyun du 'o/_/zhes _sa tsha_gsungs so/_/kun tu bzang mo klong gsal 'bar ma nyi ma'i gsang rgyud las/_a nu'i theg pa bstan pa'i le'u ste zhe bzhi pa'o// _brda' yig :

[CHAPTER 50]_ ston pas yang 'di skad gsung /_snod dang mi ldan slob ma ni/_/rigs ngan blo chung ngang rgyud thung /_/kha zol shes chung gdung ltas che/_/kha mkhas lag dam g.yo zog che//bla ma'i gsung gcog drin lan rtsod/_/yon tan mi mthong skyon la rtogs/_/rigs rgyud ngang rgyud ngan pa dang /_bka' drin khyad bsad rang la bstod/_/dam tshig nyams len phyal bar btang /_/de lta bu'i gang zag la/_/rdzogs pa chen po'i don mi bstan/_/bla ma smad dam thabs kyi gsang /_/rang gis che ba gzhog ngom byed/_/gdams ngag zab mo zin ris _rgyu byed|_|dpe rkun khram pa stong mi thub/_/blo rgod 'ur 'grogs blo gtad med/_/don dam dam tshig phyal bar btang /_chang dbang gnyid dang le lor btang /_/sgrub pa g.yel cing mu med g.yeng /_/gdong du bstod cing lkog shub smra/_/thabs dang g.yo'i gdams pa 'bru/_/rang gi nyams su ma blangs pa/_/gzhan la dbang khrid ston par rings/_/mi 'go bskor [155] 'dod rang mgo bskor/_/ de 'dra'i snod ngan 'phrad pa na/_/slob ma ma brtag bla ma'i dgra/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa'i dgra bo yin/_/de las gdams ngag gi 'brel mi bya/_/gal te gdams pa byin pa na/_/dug can snod dang zhabs rdol dang /_/rdza so ma btang spyad pa 'dra/_/snod chag bcud 'bo don mi 'grub/_/snod dang mi ldan gdams pa spel/_/rdo rje'i dmyal bar ltung bar 'gyur/_/zhes gsungs so/_/kun tu bzang mo klong gsal 'bar ma nyi ma'i gsang rgyud las/_slob ma ngan pa spang ba'i le'u ste lnga bcu pa'o// brda' yig : 

[CHAPTER 51] kun bzang yum gyi yang gsungs pa/_/bla ma ma brtag slob ma'i dgra/_/dmyal bar khrid pa'i lam mkhan yin/_/gal te 'phrad pa'i nyen yod pas/_/mtshan nyid 'di ltar shes par bya/_/bla ma zhes pa'i ming yang btags/_/brgyud pa'i byin brlab bka' bab med/_/gdams ngag yod zer tshod dpag ston/_/'dul khrims med pa khyim pa'i gzugs|_|lha chos bor nas mi chos kyi/_/so nam bu smad gsog 'jog rem/_/rang la nyams len yon tan med/_/gzhan la log lta spyod log ston/_/rigs dang brgyud pa nga che [156] zer|_|spyod pa khyi phag las kyang lod/_/dregs pa che 'dod ming che la/_/stong sob rdzun la mi tshe bskyal/_/sa ris bdag 'dzin ris su bcad/_/gson gshin log pa'i lam du khrid |_|rgyu 'bras khyad bsad kha lta mtho'/_/chang nag nyid la bsgrub pa byed/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa'i srog la bsdos/_/snying rje med cing chags sdang che/_/nyag gcig 'khor 'das _rgyu kun gyi gzhi/_/rang byung ye shes rang las byung /_/de shes ye shes rtsal yin te/_/de lta bu'i zur ma go/_/mi mgo bskor cing rang don bsgrub/_/gdul bya'i bstan 'dzin zog la_byed|_|chos rgyus med pas mkhas drung bshol/_/mi shes blun po'i tshogs rnams la/_/nga che chos bshad kha tsho 'don/_/khyi skyag sbrang ma 'du ba ltar/_/tshogs ma bsags pa'i bla ma la|_|las ngan can gyi 'khor gyis bskor/_/bzhed pa mtho ris sangs rgyas bzhed/_/gshegs pa na raka dmyal bar gshegs/_/long bas long ba khrid pa 'dra/_/be'u sbrel g.yang la lhung ba 'dra/_/mtshan nyid mi ldan bla ma yis/_/dbang bskur byas kyang gnyis ka phung /_/tha mal log par khrid pa la/_ngan song min pa 'gro sa med/_/de 'dra mi gtsang bum pa [157] la|_|bzang bzang 'dra yang ma 'brel cig_/dam pa'i chos kyis rgyang thag bsring /_/phyi bltas bzang bzang 'dra mod kyang /_/nang skyon khong nas brdog tsam na|_|nam phug skyon cig cis kyang 'ong /_/dam nyams gnyis ka dmyal bar 'gro/_/des na thog mar brtags par bya'o/_/zhes gsungs so/_/kun tu bzang mo klong gsal 'bar ma nyi ma'i gsang rgyud las/_bla ma ngan pa'i mtshan nyid bstan pa'i le'u ste nga gcig pa'o//_brda' yig : 

[CHAPTER 52] yang cig ston pas bka' stsal pa/_/bsten bya'i bla ma rnyed pa dang /_/snod _rdzo dang ldan pa'i slob bu des/_/gus pas 'di ltar bsten par bya/_/ngang lhod sems dal skabs btsal la/_/bla
